## ile_bact_B_thailandensis

This record seems to be incorrectly translated from
nucleotides to amino acids. Variation up to 5.00% is
tolerated by the script but the variation in this
translation is 94.07%.

Additionally, taking the reverse complement
of the nucleotide sequence still results in a variation
of 94.18%.

## ile_bact_D_radiodurans

This record seems to be incorrectly translated from
nucleotides to amino acids. Variation up to 5.00% is
tolerated by the script but the variation in this
translation is 92.76%.

Additionally, taking the reverse complement
of the nucleotide sequence still results in a variation
of 94.43%.

## leu_bact_G_obscuriglobus

This record seems to be incorrectly translated from
nucleotides to amino acids. Variation up to 5.00% is
tolerated by the script but the variation in this
translation is 93.16%.

Additionally, taking the reverse complement
of the nucleotide sequence still results in a variation
of 94.46%.

## val_bact_T_maritima

This record seems to be incorrectly translated from
nucleotides to amino acids. Variation up to 5.00% is
tolerated by the script but the variation in this
translation is 93.53%.

Additionally, taking the reverse complement
of the nucleotide sequence still results in a variation
of 94.45%.
